msg:A hotel in the Kaiyuan series, quite satisfied.
The price is 318 including breakfast, breakfast for 1.4 children is charged 39 yuan. The price is cheaper than the official booking of Kaiyuan. The breakfast for two at Baidawu is more than 390.
1. It doesn't feel like a downtown area, it's in the suburbs, anyway, it doesn't matter if you're just passing by and playing in the city center.
2. The hotel breakfast is OK, and it's rich for this price.
3. The room is not too big or small, and the decoration is OK.
There are quite a lot of weddings and banquets here during the May Day holidays, and I guess the locals like this place.
The parking lot is quite large. The next day, I went to the Railway Guerrilla Memorial Hall (separate, not the one on Weishan Island, Weishan Lake), and then went to Weishan Island. The 126 yuan discount ticket is OK (ticket plus ferry plus island sightseeing bus). Flat

posted:Posted February 17, 2024
msg:The hotel is located next to Guishan Park, not far from the city government, but very quiet. It may be a new district (because I am not familiar with the geographical location when I come here for the first time), and it is a good place for leisure and vacation. The ground parking lot is large and convenient for parking. Judging from the decoration style and facilities of the room, it should not have been opened for a long time. The room is clean and sanitary, the bedding is comfortable, and yogurt and fruit are provided after check-in. It is particularly worth mentioning that the restaurant provides a reasonably priced dinner service with local specialties of Zaozhuang. In addition, the breakfast is particularly rich, combining Chinese and Western styles, especially various pasta, local specialties, etc. The disadvantage is that the house I live in is on the second floor, and the bathroom has an unpleasant smell.
